			return this.1FFDCE();

		temp = A - 0x02;
		
		if (Z == 1)
			return this.1FFDDD();

		temp = A - 0x03;
		
		if (Z == 1)
			return this.1FFDEC();

		P &= ~0x20;
		A = 0x0000;
		[0x1F35] = A;
		A = 0x0000;
		[0x1F37] = A;
		return;
	}

	public void 1FFDCE()
	{
		P &= ~0x20;
		A = 0x0000;
		[0x1F35] = A;
		A = 0x0100;
		[0x1F37] = A;
		return;
	}

	public void 1FFDDD()
	{
		P &= ~0x20;
		A = 0x0100;
		[0x1F35] = A;
		A = 0x0000;
		[0x1F37] = A;
		return;
	}

	public void 1FFDEC()
	{
		P &= ~0x20;
		A = 0x0100;
		[0x1F35] = A;
		A = 0x0100;
		[0x1F37] = A;
		return;
	}

	public void 1FFDFB()
	{
		Stack.Push(P);
		P |= 0x20;
		P &= ~0x10;
		X = 0x0060;
	}

	public void 1FFE03()
	{
		A = [0x1FFE1E + X];
		[0x000101 + X] = A;
		X--;
		
		if (N == 0)
			return this.1FFE03();

		X = 0x59C1;
	}

	public void 1FFE11()
	{
		A = [0x028000 + X];
		[0x7E3193 + X] = A;
		X--;
		
		if (N == 0)
			return this.1FFE11();

		P = Stack.Pop();
		return;
	}

	public void 7E33BA()
	{
		Cpu.Break();
	}

	public void 7E4EE9()
	{
		Cpu.Break();
	}

	public void 7E4F10()
	{
		Cpu.Break();
	}
